<P style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:-2px; width:48px; font-size:11pt; 
float:left"><B>2.</B></P>
<P style="margin:0px; padding-left:48px; text-indent:-2px; font-
size:11pt"><B>Date of Material Change:</B></P>
<P style="margin:0px; clear:left"><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0px; padding-left:48px; font-size:11pt">August 8, 2016</P>
<P style="margin:0px"><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:-2px; width:48px; font-size:11pt; 
float:left"><B>3.</B></P>
<P style="margin:0px; padding-left:48px; text-indent:-2px; font-
size:11pt"><B>News Release:</B></P>
<P style="margin:0px; clear:left" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0px; padding-left:48px; padding-right:4.933px; font-size:11pt" 
align=justify>On August 8, 2016, the Company issued a news release reporting the
material change through Canada News Wire.</P>
<P style="margin:0px"><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:-2px; width:48px; font-size:11pt; 
float:left"><B>4.</B></P>
<P style="margin:0px; padding-left:48px; text-indent:-2px; font-
size:11pt"><B>Summary of Material Change:</B></P>
<P style="margin:0px; clear:left" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0px; padding-left:48px; padding-right:4.933px; font-size:11pt" 
align=justify>On August 8, 2016, the Company announced it had changed its name 
to Fiore Exploration Ltd. and announced its new stock symbol and CUSIP 
number.</P>
<P style="margin:0px"><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:-2px; width:48px; font-size:11pt; 
float:left"><B>5.</B></P>
<P style="margin:0px; padding-left:48px; text-indent:-2px; font-
size:11pt"><B>Full Description of Material Change:</B></P>
<P style="margin:0px; clear:left" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0px; padding-left:48px; padding-right:4.933px; font-size:11pt" 
align=justify>On August 8, 2016, the Company announced that effective at the 
opening Monday, August 8, 2016, the common shares of Fiore Exploration Ltd., new
stock symbol TSXV:F, will commence trading on the TSX Venture Exchange, and the 
common shares of Rouge Resources Ltd., old stock symbol ROU.V, will be delisted.
&nbsp;In connection with the name change the Company advised of its new CUSIP 
number of 31809M 10 9.</P>
<P style="margin:0px"><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:-2px; width:48px; font-size:11pt; 
float:left"><B>6.</B></P>
<P style="margin:0px; padding-left:48px; text-indent:-2px; font-
size:11pt"><B>Reliance on subsection 7.1(2) of National Instrument 51-
102:</B></P>
<P style="margin:0px; clear:left"><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0px; padding-left:48px; font-size:11pt">Not applicable.</P>
<P style="margin:0px"><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:-2px; width:48px; font-size:11pt; 
float:left"><B>7.</B></P>
<P style="margin:0px; padding-left:48px; text-indent:-2px; font-
size:11pt"><B>Omitted Information:</B></P>
<P style="margin:0px; clear:left"><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0px; padding-left:48px; font-size:11pt">No significant facts 
otherwise required to be disclosed in this report have been omitted.</P>
<P style="margin:0px"><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:-2px; width:48px; font-size:11pt;

<P style="margin:0px"><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0px; font-family:Calibri,Times New Roman; font-size:14pt" 
align=center><B>FIORE EXPLORATION LTD. ANNOUNCES PRIVATE PLACEMENT</B></P>
<P style="margin:0px" align=center><BR></P>
<TABLE style="margin-top:0px; font-size:10pt" cellpadding=0 cellspacing=0 
width=100%><TR height=0 style="font-size:0"><TD /><TD width=300.533 /></TR>

</TD><TD style="margin-top:0px" valign=top width=300.533><P style="margin:0px;

F</B></P>
</TD></TR>
</TABLE>
<P style="margin:0px" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0px; font-family:Calibri,Times New Roman; font-size:11pt" 
align=justify>VANCOUVER, B.C., August 12, 2016 &#150; Fiore Exploration Ltd. 
(&#147;Fiore Ex&#148; or the &#147;Company&#148;) (TSXV: F), announces a non-
brokered private placement of 12,750,000 common shares at a price of $0.55 per 
common share, for gross proceeds of $7,012,500. &nbsp;&nbsp;The private 
placement has been fully allocated and remains subject to the approval of the 
TSX Venture Exchange.</P>
<P style="margin:0px"><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0px; font-family:Calibri,Times New Roman; font-size:11pt" 
align=justify>Tim Warman, P.Geo., Fiore&#146;s CEO, is the Qualified Person who 
supervised the preparation of the technical data in this news release.</P>
<P style="margin:0px"><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0px; font-family:Calibri,Times New Roman; font-
size:11pt"><B>ABOUT FIORE EXPLORATION LTD.</B></P>
<P style="margin:0px; font-family:Calibri,Times New Roman; font-size:11pt" 
align=justify>Fiore Exploration Ltd., has acquired the Pampas El Pe&#241;on gold
project in Chile from Arena Minerals, a project which covers land in the same 
geological environment as Yamana's flagship El Pe&#241;on mine. </P>
<P style="margin:0px"><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0px; font-family:Calibri,Times New Roman; font-size:11pt"><B>On
behalf of FIORE EXPLORATION LTD.</B></P>
<P style="margin:0px"><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0px; font-family:Calibri,Times New Roman; font-
size:11pt">&quot;Tim Warman&quot; </P>
<P style="margin:0px; font-family:Calibri,Times New Roman; font-size:11pt">Chief
Executive Officer</P>
<P style="margin:0px"><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0px; font-family:Calibri,Times New Roman; font-size:11pt">For 
further information please contact: &nbsp;604-609-6110</P>
<P style="margin:0px"><BR></P>

</TD><TD style="margin-top:0px" valign=top width=300.533><P style="margin:0px;

<P style="margin:0px" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0px; font-family:Calibri,Times New Roman; font-size:11pt" 
align=justify>VANCOUVER, B.C., August 12, 2016 &#150; Fiore Exploration Ltd. 
(&#147;Fiore Ex&#148; or the &#147;Company&#148;) (TSXV: F), announces that 
further to this morning&#146;s new release it has increased the non-brokered 
private placement to 18,200,000 common shares at a price of $0.55 per common 
share, for gross proceeds of $10,010,000. &nbsp;&nbsp;The private placement has 
been fully allocated and remains subject to the approval of the TSX Venture 
Exchange.</P>
<P style="margin:0px" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0px; font-family:Calibri,Times New Roman; font-size:11pt" 
align=justify>Tim Warman, P.Geo., Fiore&#146;s CEO, is the Qualified Person who 
supervised the preparation of the technical data in this news release.</P>
<P style="margin:0px" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0px; font-family:Calibri,Times New Roman; font-size:11pt" 
align=justify><B>ABOUT FIORE EXPLORATION LTD.</B></P>
<P style="margin:0px; font-family:Calibri,Times New Roman; font-size:11pt" 
align=justify>Fiore Exploration Ltd., has acquired the Pampas El Pe&#241;on gold
project in Chile from Arena Minerals, a project which covers land in the same 
geological environment as Yamana's flagship El Pe&#241;on mine. </P>
<P style="margin:0px" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0px; font-family:Calibri,Times New Roman; font-size:11pt" 
align=justify><B>On behalf of FIORE EXPLORATION LTD.</B></P>
<P style="margin:0px" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0px; font-family:Calibri,Times New Roman; font-size:11pt" 
align=justify>&quot;Tim Warman&quot; </P>
<P style="margin:0px; font-family:Calibri,Times New Roman; font-size:11pt" 
align=justify>Chief Executive Officer</P>
<P style="margin:0px" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0px; font-family:Calibri,Times New Roman; font-size:11pt" 
align=justify>For further information please contact: &nbsp;604-609-6110</P>
<P style="margin:0px" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0px; font-family:Calibri,Times New Roman" 
align=justify><I>Neither the TSX Venture Exchange nor its Regulation Services 
Provider (as that term is defined in the policies of the TSX Venture Exchange) 
accepts responsibility for the adequacy or accuracy of this release.</I></P>
